                      <div data-reactid="314">
                       The ROOM: has a twin size bed with a small armoire, and the bed has three drawers. Upon request, sleep to the sound of the fountain near by. BATHROOMS: You'll be sharing a one and a half (1 1/2 bathrooms). LOCATION: Located in historic Garvanza District, the borderline between South Pasadena and Highland Park. It is conveniently located 10 driving minutes from downtown Los Angeles by the 110 Freeway (a historic parkway called Arroyo Seco Prkwy), Pasadena, and San Marino. It is about 8 miles from JPL (Jet Propulsion Laboratory-NASA) and within walking distance from the Rose Bowl. TRANSPORTATION: The Dash stops near our property, and 1 mile from the "Highland Park" Metro Station (Line: Golden Line). Local stores and restaurants are all within walking distance. SPECIAL: Garvanza District: considered a sub district of Highland Park, got its name for the wild sweet peas, i.e. garbanzo beans that used to grow on the hillsides. Garvanza District was the heart of the Arts and Crafts movement in Los Angeles and a bohemian artists' colony, and is today one of Northeast LA's hidden treasures. This small and hilly area filled with historic buildings has more than enough charm and character needed to stand out on its own. PLACES NEAR US YOU MAY WANT TO VISIT: The Rose Bowl The Tournament of Roses Parade Chinatown Little Tokyo Placita Olvera MOCA Norton Simon Museum Dodger Stadium Staples Center Old Town Pasadena Universal Studios Griffith Park Southwest Museum Huntington Libray and Gardens JPL Judson Studios L.A. Opera at Dorothy Chandler Pavilion Walt Disney Concert Hall The Hollywood Bowl Griffith Observatory L.A. Zoo Hollywood Walk of Fame Universal Studios NATURE LOVERS: Wild Life: You will see birds coming to feed and bathe, hummingbirds, and even if you're lucky a squirrel coming into our backyard or a monarch butterfly or two. NATURE TRAIL: The Arroyo Seco Trail close by is a nice quiet walk or for jogging along side nature and its wild life which is about 15 minutes walk from our house.The trail ends at the Rose Bowl. On this trail, you may observe hawks, docks, geese, rabbits and even a coyote! HORSE LOVERS: Right along the trail sits an old Horse Stable, with some enclosures. . GOLF COURSE AND TENNIS COURTS: Brookside Golf Club designed by famed golf architect William P. Bell, has 36 holes and is nestled in the golden foothills of Pasadena next to the world famous Rose Bowl is only 5 to 7 minutes drive. Also a nine-hole golf course and tennis courts are within walking distance of our home The HOUSE: Our house has a large four- tier back yard (No railings) and a small front yard. The peaceful backyard has plenty of space for relaxing while listening to the water fountain in the small pond, sun bathing, or simply reading a good book. We have a 12' X 30" above ground Intex pool. LIVING ROOM: There is a comfortable cozy living room with a wood burning fireplace. The DINING ROOM: which is adjacent to the kitchen, accommodates six people. There is a small family room with a large TV. PARKING: There is unrestricted street parking available in front of our house.
                      </div>
                      <div data-reactid="315">
                       "Once the heart of the Arts and Crafts movement in Los Angeles and a bohemian artists' colony, Garvanza is today one of Northeast LA's hidden treasures seeking to retain its turn of the century identity while creating a liveable neighborhood for the twenty-first century. Although many consider Garvanza to be just a part of Highland Park, this small and hilly area brimming with historic buildings has more than enough charm and character needed to stand out on its own. Named for the wild sweet peas (garbanzo beans) that used to grow on the hillsides, Garvanza itself is much like a hearty wildflower, blooming stubbornly amidst the dominant concreted landscape, unabashedly colorful and pleasantly surprising to discover.:" (URL HIDDEN)
                      </div>
                      <div data-reactid="316">
                       <li data-reactid="317"><p data-reactid="318">Ann-Marie and Emeric are so friendly and cooperative, when i arrived at their beautiful house i found my room is clean and prepared, it was exactly as it appeared in the photos. we spent a lot of time chatting and eating together, Emeric took me and showed me the nearby places, they are open minded and like to explore different cultures. The neighbourhood is clean and safe, DASH bus stop is directly in front of their house and it takes you to Highland park Metro station, a lot of other different buses pass near to the area. Really, with them i felt like i'm at home.</p><span data-reactid="319">Amr</span><span data-reactid="320">2015-01-16T00:00:00Z</span></li>
                       <li data-reactid="321"><p data-reactid="322">This is my first time with Airbnb. I lived here for 3 months during the summer. The room was very small and is on the first floor. The bathroom is near the kitchen and the shower is on the second floor. With no air conditioner, the heat in the room was extreme and unbearable during the day and sometimes even at night. I often saw ants in the house including my bedroom. Street parking was often difficult to find and the area didn’t feel safe for overnight parking. The hosts had several written rules to follow like no food in the bedroom, cleaning the dishes after use, and so on. They also had unwritten rules like maximum 10-minute shower and only 2 loads of laundry per week. At the beginning, I felt the hosts were pleasant, but later on I felt differently. When I come back from work, I really prefer to relax and have quiet alone time. The male host wanted to have conversation with me and, at times, I felt that he was asking too many questions which kind of turned into long discussions. I really didn’t feel like talking to him at all, so I tried to avoid him at all cost, but since I have to eat in the kitchen area and pass through the common area for bathroom and shower, I constantly ran into him. I tried to avoid him even to a point of not greeting him in fear that he might want to carry on a conversation. He gave me a pep talk about me not saying hi, so we agreed to just greet each other and have no further discussion. That ended shortly after he broke the agreement by asking me more questions. I felt the hosts think that the guest has to socialize with them; I believe I am just renting a place to rest in privacy. I didn’t think it was necessary to have to be so social with people that I’m not particularly close with, over boundaries that I didn’t really wish to cross. I guess there is difference in opinion. Two days before the end of my planned stay, which was fully paid for, my family came by to help me pack. The male host started to yell at me and my family about my behavior and not greeting him. Eventually, we apologized and ended the argument, but he continued and became more hostile and said a racially derogatory remark. My parents felt that it was not safe to leave their daughter here, so they decided to finish packing and leave the place right away. So I left two days before the scheduled leave. The hosts should make the rules clear in advance and not make it up as you go. Overall, my experience was not what I expected, and I definitely would not use this place again. </p><span data-reactid="323">Tiffany</span><span data-reactid="324">2016-09-05T00:00:00Z</span></li>

                      <div data-reactid="1029">
                       A private tranquil retreat in an Architect's Guest House awaits you only 10 minutes from downtown Los Angeles and nearby Pasadena Cal Tech and Occidental College. This unique guesthouse is nestled under an enormous oak tree shaded in a secluded garden located behind the Architect's main house. Easy off street parking. Discover our nearby exciting and eclectic shops, restaurants, gastro pubs and bars along Highland Park's artsy vibrant and ever-changing York Blvd &amp; Figueroa St.
                      </div>
                      <div data-reactid="1030">
                       Newly constructed architecturally designed tranquil, spacious, airy and bright retreat. Totally private self self contained unit with full kitchen, bathroom, vaulted ceiling with operable skylights, smart tv, large closet and private patio and gated secure entry. You enter this romantic garden retreat through a locked gate at the end of the driveway. Upon entering, one walks down the security lite driveway past the front of the garage and down the deck through the garden following the deck to the rear private guest house entry. There are three-way exterior lights along the deck-way to the entrance. Once inside lighting and environmental controls are on the left as you enter the main space of the guest house. There you can switch off the exterior lights and switch on your interior ones. The skylight is perfect for couples desiring privacy and intimate surroundings. There is an additional couch bed that opens into a twin size bed for an additional family member or friend. It has a queen size bed and memory foam mattress, large closet, and drawers. The operable skylights allow guests to enjoy windows have curtains and light blocking screens that insure a good nights sleep. It is a quiet, tranquil room generously spacious for two people.
                      </div>
                      <div data-reactid="1031">
                       A very quiet and peaceful neighborhood located on a street and block that ends in a cul-de-sac. Outside of our quite street down York Blvd. or on Figueroa Street you will discover our exciting multiethnic, cosmopolitan and lively Highland Park commercial areas with great restaurants, bars and shops. There are a couple of neighborhood restaurants and food trucks conveniently located in walking distance to our home. Many more restaurants and bars are located nearby in Highland Park, South Pasadena, Pasadena, Eagle Rock and Downtown LA. Our home is also conveniently located near Occidental College, Cal Tech, and JPL, The Jet Propulsion Laboratory.

                      <div data-reactid="1734">
                       Your oasis is secluded at the end of a hardwood hallway with a Queen sized bed and views of the uninhabited rolling hills and canyons. Listen at night for faint sounds of the great horned owls in the distance. A very quiet and serene place to be. All our rooms are immaculate. We LOVE CLEAN and hope you do too.
                      </div>
                      <div data-reactid="1735">
                       We're in the hills above the Pasadena Rose Bowl Stadium, close to the Pasadena Convention Center and within walking distance to hiking trails overlooking JPL and La Cañada. As part of a four floor 1928 multi-million dollar gated estate the grounds on a clear day reveal a glimpse of the ocean in the distance. Within walking distance are hiking trails into the canyons. This Spanish Mediterranean estate was originally built by two women from Chicago in the roaring 20’s. The home is on the national register of historic places and is particularly noted for its rare collection of 1920‘s Batchelder tile. Mr. Batchelder was a famous maker of art tiles and leader of the American Arts and Crafts Movement as well as founder of the Pasadena Playhouse. The hand-made tiles while typically only found sparingly used around fireplaces abound in the Great Room of the home with an entire floor made of this rare and unique tile. ..::: As seen in the photos :::.. the home contains curiosities from around the globe. Visual delights are everywhere from a massive Indian “floating door” in the living room to Mughal empire inspired tapestry crafted of golden thread and semi-precious stones of Kashmiri origin. Ancient thrown pots from Israel sit atop intricately carved wooden columns surrounded by Brazilian antiques nestled within a 35 foot high cathedral ceiling. A 12th Century Cambodian Apsara the female spirit of the clouds and waters quietly bemuse our guests while Moroccan glow lanterns adorn Persian artifacts and antique tea pots on display. Have your morning tea or coffee outside on the veranda overlooking Los Angeles with a delightfully friendly but exotic Black Russian Terrier. This is a quiet serene place of reflection, rebirth and rejuvenation.
                      </div>
                      <div data-reactid="1736">
                       Ruby-throated hummingbirds, wild parrots and Great Horned Owls in the evening abound naturally in this completely gated magical yet majestic setting. Extraordinarily quiet this home overlooking the Annandale golf course and views of the city is a place to relax in the evenings next to the outdoor fire place chimenea and take in the spectacular sunsets with a glass of wine or sun tea. We are close to the Pasadena Rose Bowl as well as the Pasadena Convention Center. The estate in the past has been both a filming location, as well as a backdrop to international model celebrity shoots and host to multiple fund-raising events with indoor/outdoor cocktail parties exceeding a guest list of over 100 on special request.
                      </div>

                      <div data-reactid="1862">
                       LOCATION: in historic Garvanza District, the borderline between South Pasadena and Highland Park. It is conveniently located 10 driving minutes from downtown Los Angeles by the 110 Freeway (a historic parkway called Arroyo Seco Prkwy), Pasadena, and San Marino. It is less than 8 miles from JPL (Jet Propulsion Laboratory-NASA) and withing walking distance from the Rose Bowl. TRANSPORTATION: The Dash stops two houses down from our property, and 1 mile from Highland Park station of the Metro Golden Line. Local stores and restaurants are all within walking distance. The AREA: Garvanza District: considered a sub district of Highland Park, got its name for the wild sweet peas, i.e. garbanzo beans that used to grow on the hillsides. SPECIAL: Garvanza District was the heart of the Arts and Crafts movement in Los Angeles and a bohemian artists' colony, and is today one of Northeast LA's hidden treasures. This small and hilly area filled with historic buildings has more than enough charm and character needed to stand out on its own. TRANSPORTATION: The Dash stops near our property, and 1 mile from the "Highland Park" Metro Station (Line: Golden Line). Local stores and restaurants are all within walking distance. Opera at Dorothy Chandler Pavilion Walt Disney Concert Hall The Hollywood Bowl Griffith Observatory L.A. Zoo Hollywood Walk of Fame Universal Studios NATURE LOVERS: Wild Life: You will see birds coming to feed and bathe, hummingbirds, and even if you're lucky a squirrel coming into our backyard or a monarch butterfly or two. NATURE TRAIL: The Arroyo Seco Trail close by is a nice quiet walk or for jogging along side nature and its wild life which is about 15 minutes walk from our house.The trail ends at the Rose Bowl. On this trail, you may observe hawks, docks, geese, rabbits and even a coyote! HORSE LOVERS: Right along the trail sits an old Horse Stable, with some enclosures. . GOLF COURSE AND TENNIS COURTS: Brookside Golf Club designed by famed golf architect William P. Bell, has 36 holes and is nestled in the golden foothills of Pasadena next to the world famous Rose Bowl is only 5 to 7 minutes drive. Also a nine-hole golf course and tennis courts are within walking distance of our home The HOUSE: Our house has a big four- tier back yard (no railings) and a small front yard. The backyard has plenty of space for relaxing while listening to the water fountain in the small pond, sun bathing, or simply reading a good book. LIVING ROOM: There is a comfortable cozy living room with a wood burning fireplace. The DINING ROOM: is adjacent to the kitchen, accommodates six people. There is a small family room with a large TV. PARKING: There is unrestricted street parking available in front of our house.

This Spanish Mediterranean estate was originally built by two women from Chicago in the roaring 20’s. The home is on the national register of historic places and is particularly noted for its rare collection of 1920‘s Batchelder tile.  Mr. Batchelder was a famous maker of art tiles and leader of the American Arts and Crafts Movement as well as founder of the Pasadena Playhouse. The hand-made tiles while typically only found sparingly used around fireplaces abound in the Great Room of the home with an entire floor made of this rare and unique tile.\n..::: As seen in the photos :::..  the home contains curiosities from around the globe.
